<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заражать.html>заража́ть</a> (26447)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заразить.html>зарази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zarazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заражать.html>заража́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaražátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заразить.html>зарази́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to infect</li>
<li>to contaminate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заражать.html>заража́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>во́ду</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaražátʹ</b> vódu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to infect/contaminate/poison/pollute water</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заражаться.html>заража́ться</a> (26010)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заражать.html>заража́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaražátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заражаться.html>заража́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaražátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заразиться.html>зарази́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to catch, to contract, to be infected <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заражаться.html>заража́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaražátʹsja</b> ot kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get the infection [contract the disease] from smb</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заражаться.html>заража́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грипп.html>гри́ппом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaražátʹsja</b> gríppom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to catch/contract flu/grippe</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(emotions, mood, ideas etc)</i> to be infected/contaminated <i>(with, by)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заражаться.html>заража́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:всеобщий.html>всео́бщим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:энтузиазм.html>энтузиа́змом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaražátʹsja</b> vseóbščim entuziázmom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be infected by [caught up in] everybody's enthusiasm</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заражаться.html>заража́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́выми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взгляд.html>взгля́дами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaražátʹsja</b> právymi vzgljádami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be contaminated by right-wing ideas</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заражать.html>заража́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaražátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:инфицирование.html>инфици́рование</a></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зараза.html>зара́за</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaráza</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зараза.html>зара́зы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зараза.html>зара́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зараза.html>зара́з</a></b>)

***заразительный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заразительный.html>зарази́тельный</a> (18307)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заразить.html>зарази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zarazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заразительный.html>зарази́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarazítelʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)зарази́тельнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)зарази́тельней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also  figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> infectious, contagious</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разить.html>рази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to reek</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заразить.html>зарази́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarazítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заражать.html>заража́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to infect</li>
<li>to contaminate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заразить.html>зарази́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>во́ду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zarazítʹ</b> vódu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to infect/contaminate/poison/pollute water</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заразиться.html>зарази́ться</a> (18073)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заразить.html>зарази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zarazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заразиться.html>зарази́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarazítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заражаться.html>заража́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to catch, to contract, to be infected <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заразиться.html>зарази́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zarazítʹsja</b> ot kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get the infection [contract the disease] from smb</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заразиться.html>зарази́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грипп.html>гри́ппом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zarazítʹsja</b> gríppom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to catch/contract flu/grippe</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(emotions, mood, ideas etc)</i> to be infected/contaminated <i>(with, by)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заразиться.html>зарази́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:всеобщий.html>всео́бщим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:энтузиазм.html>энтузиа́змом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zarazítʹsja</b> vseóbščim entuziázmom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be infected by [caught up in] everybody's enthusiasm</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заразиться.html>зарази́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́выми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взгляд.html>взгля́дами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zarazítʹsja</b> právymi vzgljádami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be contaminated by right-wing ideas</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заразить.html>зарази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zarazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зарастать.html>зараста́ть</a> (23772)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарасти.html>зарасти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zarastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарастать.html>зараста́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarastátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарасти.html>зарасти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be overgrown, to be covered with vegetation, to hair, to fur, etc.</li>
<li>to heal, to skin over (of a wound)</li></ol>

***зарегистрироваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зарегистрироваться.html>зарегистри́роваться</a> (22675)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарегистрировать.html>зарегистри́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaregistrírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарегистрироваться.html>зарегистри́роваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaregistrírovatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регистрироваться.html>регистри́роваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to register oneself</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to register one's marriage</li>

***зарезать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зарезать.html>зареза́ть</a> (6680)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резать.html>ре́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарезать.html>заре́зать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarézatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарезать.html>зареза́ть</a></strong></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to stab (to death), to knife, to kill, to carve up; to butcher, to stick</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to axe, to kill (a part in a play, a bill, etc.)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарезать.html>заре́зать</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zarézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарезать.html>зареза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarezátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарезать.html>заре́зать</a></strong></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зарекомендовать.html>зарекомендова́ть</a> (25538)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рекомендовать.html>рекомендова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rekomendovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарекомендовать.html>зарекомендова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarekomendovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зарекомендо́вывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to prove to be, to turn out (a particular way)</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">решети́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rešetítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (end-stressed) or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">реше́тить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rešétitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (stem-stressed).

***зародиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зародиться.html>зароди́ться</a> (15558)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">зароди́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zarodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зародиться.html>зароди́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarodítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарождаться.html>зарожда́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be conceived</li>
<li>to arise, to be born
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зародиться.html>зароди́лось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сомнение.html>сомне́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>zarodílosʹ</b> somnénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a doubt arose in his mind; he began to feel doubtful</span></div></dd></dl></li>
